juego violento con signos y símbolos, letras o colores o
expresando nada más lo que la suma de todas las palabras
su resto su división meticulosa desde cuantas perspectivas
sea posible: ambivalencia, no expresa nada, y si lo
hiciera, no importaria. el argumento no es más que una
pesada roca con un símbolo tallado en su centro,
una herramienta a usar sólo en determinado momento del año.
estos medios, lenguaje, pincel, arte-interactivo-multimedia-blablabla,
son totalmente maleables, like glue.
ascii, retrato de una abstracción. arte no matemático, o
matemática de lo irracional little green numbers all over the room.
aberración que sintetiza ideas de cocteau y steve jobs y la idea
principal la única que persiste en este arte post-post-post-moderno:
síntesis, contradicción, absurdo. rebelión post-modem, venganza
violenta si es necesario.
tiene que ser espontáneo claro; y rápido
. no espera ni recibe, y es abierto. algo se cierra
con cada lectura pero se niega a cerrarse por completo
el modernismo fue engengrado bajo un sueño de
láudano de coleridge transmitido a verlain mallarmé
por una línea dorada como en oriente;
esto no es ningún sueño nada nos caracteriza
sin posibilidad de hacento horizontal ni vertical
ninguna droga es nuestra todas lo son
sólo la decadencia y una bola de nieve que cae en el desierto
inclinaciones? claro que hacia toda corriente estética
irracional, el naturalismo es aburrido porque cree tener
importancia: sabemos que no tenemos nada que decir.
el realismo brillante de los espejos de agua, sería tonto limitarnos.
así como argumento y sentido, cualquier tipo de valor
en la obra, calidad cualquier piedrita-en-el-camino o regla,
estética o moral, es innecesaria y accesorio;
una personita -haciendo- es piedra suficiente.
en el escenario hay una pequeña mesa, de luz, de madera;
un rompecabezas en él, está armado pero le faltan algunas piezas
y el rompecabezas es grande. parecería que deliberadamente
le sacaron esas piezas.


\\\\\\ \                \       \       \                       \       \\ \_







































Esta la acci¢n de la lluvia,
        esta la accion de quien
                permanece sentado sin dar palabra ni se¤a
                        de su existencia,
 esta quien calla a proposito en busca de algo inexistente pero que,
                a rasgos frios (la cara golpeando el vidrio que se moja
                        con la gota que moja el vidrio que se-moja con la
                        gota que golpea el vidrio plus relampago y se moja
        con la gota del),
                                vale en algo la pena.

                                esta la accion
                                        de quien se pierde
                                                        divagando..
Esta la accion
        en quien bebe copas y copas
                y al ultimo paso
                        decae, se reinventa
                                        carton y quien sabe por que
                                                camina derecho a la dire cci
        on de la lluvia.

        A quien el paso del extasis algo mas le ha dejado,
                        ademas de numeros de telefono, palabras por todas
                                        partes y recuerdos,

                                                a quien el paso, a quien
la gota el camino el vidrio
        todo carcomido por la ira
                        de la Tormenta,
                                        a quien el paso acumulado
        y la respuesta
                que se cuelga
                        de una rama y otra rama que se gotean y
                                        se juntan con el vidrio que sufre
                                                        y grita sin cesar
                                                                a traves
                                de los espasmos plasmoide del origen
                                        perdido, anclado
                                                        del rumbo Inigualable
        a traves de la lluvia y la Tormenta
                        y los espamos
                                        y las gotas sobre el vidrio..




























y quien no tiene camino y se acomoda
con la -mirada fija
en aquel rincon..
*                                               *               **      *

























hay algo que no me deja tranquilo. hay algo que no calma, es la bestia tras
la calma. Es el momento en que todo se ilumina, cuando todo esta quieto y
oscuro se hace a la luz del segundo y la barra, golpea fuerte y no hay
respuesta.




















----*****\\Para nuestro caso, en especial, para nuestra deformidad, 
                                                      (orgsync@wannabi.org)
        el alma se divide en varios procesos

                        * vacio
                        * reconocimiento absurdo,
                        * pena y gloria,
                        * muerte de los ojos invisibles,
                        * desarmado,
                        * reflexion y estimulantes,
                        * rearmado
                        * cumbre de la existencia,
                        * vacio
                        * muerte.


de por si que la muerte del alma
        no el tipico conocimiento del termino muerte, va mas alla
de la leve comprension de todos nosotros.



El vacio se caracteriza por un total desinteres hacia la elementaria magica
que nos brinda la vida:

        los celestes no son celestes,
        los arboles son una mierda
        que mierda viajar en bondi
        estoy cansado y me duele
        no no no
        -gota de azufre-
        quiero AIRE
        quiero AGUA
        -no-

el vacio se dispersa, el vacio contagia a quien en posicion de contagio
se encuentre para desterrarlo del reino de la coherencia y la pseudovida
                        sana.




--El reconocimiento absurdo es un simple
                dar con quien en este mundo.

(una patada en el culo para darnos cuenta de quienes somos.)

y en la mayoria de los casos quienes predefinidos a este ciclo del alma
se encuentren
                        no es nada glorioso.

                                es todo pura catastrofe,
puro relampago pura muerte puro
                cuelgue, calor
                                de a ratos luz que
                                        concluye en
                                                        acumulacion
                                                                de los
sentidos
        en la vacija de la vida.





(La pena y la gloria),

        la gloria de nunca sobrepasa la pena del presente,
                y el futuro no muestra demasiadas posibilidades.
(actor de teatro con tendencia psicotica, fumando marihuana a las 8am
        en caballito, a cuadras de las vias y cerca de la facultad de
        filosofia y letr s.)




** MUERTE DE LOS OJOS
        INVISIBLES

                todo proceso aneuronal finaliza.
                        la plena desvarie, el existir por inercia.
(a vos tambien?)







el desarmado trae esperanzas. deshacer la esencia para quitar lo malo y
anhadir esas particulas necesarias para el goce de la buena vida y *****

El Corazón Sur 
~~~~~~~~~~~~~~ 

"Los autómatas ya se multiplican y sueñan. 
En los cafés piden con prisa algo para escribir, 
las vetas del mármol son las gráficas de su evasión 
y sus coches van solos al Bosque". 
                                     - La Revolutión Surrealiste 


El doctor lo vio venir y se reprochó por haberse quedado de guardia 
esa noche. Tristán se acercó, ya se conocían, y le dijo con  cierto 
nerviosismo: 
- Doctor, quiero que me dé un corazón, estoy cansado de bombear mis
  venas manualmente. 

El doctor, con una tono de fastidio que quería disimular respondió: 
- Mire Tristán, en este momento no tenemos en stock, la fábrica tuvo
  algunos problemas y todavía no enviaron reposiciones. 

Tristán le clavo los ojos en las orejas, en la frente enorme y gris,
en esa cara regordeta y colorada que aparecía impasible ante él y su
sufrimiento. Con furia y desilusión le increpó: 
- Y usted dice llamarse Dios?!, Llavéh y todas esas niñerías?! Es en
  verdad un fiasco, todo usted y toda la espiritualidad. 

El doctor calló, siempre calla ante los reclamos. Tristán se  calmó,
intentó un último recurso para ver si conseguía  el alivio  a  sus 
penas. Con un postrero  aliento de esperanza le  preguntó en  forma 
deferente 
- No tiene aunque sea un corazón a gas? o un cielo electrificado que
  le sobre? 

El doctor respondió lejano y seco 
-sabe usted bien que no 

Ambos quedaron en silencio, petrificados uno frente al otro. 
Inmediatamente desaparecieron y la escena quedó desierta para el 
libre albedrío del viajante, 
mientras caía el telón.

1.


I

  hombre no palabra, con ojos de jalea de jalea de jalea jalea jalea que mira
  cabezas de ovillos de viruta de alambre y jalea, mira desde ovillos, mira
  jalea.
  mastica sus dientes de porcelana, de ladrillo ceniciento, espejos desnudos,
  ingenuos, que reflejan, reverberan metálicos los pasos de la legión, legión
  de ovillos de viruta de porcelana que resuena entre paredes de ladrillos
  cenicientos.
  pero no hay respuesta, respuesta... respuestarespuestarespuestarespuesta
  inocua entre ovillos de viruta de oveja de oveja de oveja oveja que deja,
  que arrastra, que permite, que sonríe.
- pero está el amor. está la bondad -se encoje, se arrastra, sonríe- dios,
  jesús, maría, todo el rebaño -sonríe, se encoje, se arrastra- está el
  hombre -rebosa.


II

  jesús de los esperanzados, jesús del rebaño, jesús el-de-la-tele, jesús que
  grita, que expulsa, que mata. jesús de picana, legión de viruta, ovejas de
  porcelana, y su madre la puta. jesús que abraza, que ríe, que sodomiza con
  la pija de maría. mamá me ama, mamá me ama. jesús de viruta, jesús palabra,
  jesús y la reputa que te parió, jesús de procelana, mamá me ama.



2.


Austral

me vez en penumbra;
los labios morados,
sismos pequeños en la mandíbula,
la cara más pálida,
la mirada perdida, onírica.

"te ves mal, joaquín"
decis de a poquito.
"sueño", respondo.

tengo mucho sueño;
tanto que no puedo dormir.
pregunto,
           analizo,
                    respondo.
roto,
      quebrado,
                quieto,
                         tarado de tanto preguntar,
                                   analizar,
                            responder.

"te ves mal, joaquín";
resuena, rebota, reflota,
reverbera sobra la pared
y la resquebraja.

las miro gotear,
una a una se desgastan
las palabras ya resecas
de tanto mar, de tanto camino.
y desaparecen en la pared
a un paso cansino.

no me mires,
no recuerdes,
no destapes, no desates,
        no preguntes,
no me olvides.

"te ves mal, joaquín",
y el sueño ya es otro.



3.


¿me llamaste?, ¿me pensaste?
¿me pateaste, me lloraste, me vendiste?
¿mematastememeparistemecolgaste?
¿me amaste?

es probable, lo se,
                    o eso creo.
         se desprende de las paredes,
            se desprende 
                   del costado izquierdo de la pagina,
  se desprende de tu espinazo, 
                       tu falange,
                            mi omóplato
                                 y una hipoteca.
se desprende
              y gotea,
                   gotea,
           gotea y
             gotea.
         chorrea y derrocha
       mientras me llamaste.
se desprende
          y reflota,
               sostiene,
          indaga y perfora,
                sublima
            y rebota
    mientras me pensaste, me pateaste.

se desaloja y me arás las tripas
         reflota, tus ojos gimen terciopelo oscuro
se sostiene sobre tu espinazo y sobre la hipoteca,
          rebota en el correo y en el ocaso
              gotea gota a gota
                 se desagota y se sumerge

se sostiene, en eter, en sueños e indigestones
     se sostiene y enmudece
         reverbera, repite, recalca,
           gota
        a gota se expande,
               y finalmente explota.

y ensordece, y sublima, y chorrea,
  y gime,
               y ara,
                          y gotea.
meamastemematastemelloraste.
poco a poco todo es humo,
pocoapocotodoesuno.
se expande, se agota, se desaloja,
se sumerge, se duerme, reverbera y explota.
                y se seca de a poquitiiiiito,
                         gota a gota.


                                                     -krc.

      and what exactly is a dream.       _____/     _____·---»
             ____                       \\__/__      \       º
     _____**))  º                          _(_ )_     \--»__ º---·_
     \          º__             _________/ \__  /_        /  º    /____::;:;
      \___ \_     /------//__    \      /     \__/__ ___ /---------¼/.,
        /__ /___ ____·'     /     \    /---·__  ___\   /----·__         __
       __/    / ________   /       \__       //__\    /      /__  __ __/_//

                                        and what exactly is a joke.


                   _                                   __
                  \\   tHe 14 hOUr tECHNiCOLOUr dREAm   //


Early in the morning of April 29th, an exhausted Pink Floyd departed for the
Netherlands, where they were filmed for an appearance on a Dutch TV show
called 'Fan club' and played an evening gig as well. That very same night the
Pink Floyd were scheduled to close the multi-band extravaganza known in
hippie lore as the 'The 14 Hour Technicolor Dream'. They drove back from
Holland that night, doing the tedious ferry crossing over the English Channel,
stopping in briefly at Edbrooke Road, where an exhausted Jenner and Syd each
droped a tab of acid before driving to north London's Muswell Hill in their
cramped car. Like the 1965 Albert Hall poetry reading, the event marked a
turning point in the London Underground, and was indeed an epochal highlight
event of the 1960s. An estimated 7,000 punters crowded into the massive
Alexandra Palace in London, which was hired out for the night by Hoppy and
Dave Hewson. The idea of renting out the vast Alexandra Palace had been
germinating in Hoppy's mind since he had first been there when the Stones and
John Lee Hooker played in 1964. The Technicolor Dream had been envisioned by
Hoppy as a 'giant benefit against fuzz action', as the ads carried in the
Melody Maker attested. 'Fuzz action' of the sort that had attemtped to shut
down IT, and the ostensible purpose of the Technicolor Dream was to raise
funds for IT's legal defense fund. It began at 8 PM and went through the
night until 10 AM the next morning. Hoppy and Suzy Creamcheese stood at the
door, collecting tickets and, in their inimitable style, greeting everyone.
The armies of nascent hippiedom duly congregated at the gates and filed in.
Much of the audience came in ties and blazers, with a generous assortment of
kaftan and bell wearing ravers among them. For many it proved to be an
epochal experience, as they saw for the first time that they were not the
only freaks in London. Two film crews were on hand to film the proceedings.
Peter Whitehead, director of 'Tonite Let's Make Love in London', fought for
vantage points with a film crew from the BBC, who presented a live airing of
the event on BBC-2.

Indica gallery owner John Dunbar was at John Lennon's home that evening, 'We
were all down in Weybridge, and we were watching TV and suddenly saw that
this thing was going on. So we thought, fuck it, let's go! We ended up at
this place where everybody I'd ever known in my life swam before my eyes at
one time or another. All eyes were vaguely on us because we were with John
and literally saw people I'd last seen at kindergarten and hadn't seen since.'

This was perhaps the high water mark for the Underground; a party that the
Underground threw to celebrate itself. The Underground and the vibe
cultivated at UFO certainly went overground on this night, gathering momentum,
but some would argue, losing its integrity. The small London coterie would
send out ripples that would affect most of the world's young people one way
or another in the coming years, but this was to be the grand night of all
nights for the Underground. It was certainly a show of force, as Wholly
Communion had been, simply by virtue of having so many young people under
one roof. This was not a gig or mundane pop show, rather this was an event
like the poetry reading that would galvanize the Underground and bring
diverse pockets of 'freaks' and 'hippies' out of the woodwork.
Word of the event had spread throughout London, and expectations were high.
Two stages had been erected inside the cavernous hall, with a smaller central
stage designed for poets, performance artists and dancers, jugglers, the
Tribe of the Sacred Mushroom, Phillipine dancer David Medalla and the
Exploding Galaxy dance troupe. The larger stage for the main events was built
along the back wall, flanked by the large glass windows of the Palace. Jack
Henry Moore and a small army of technicians were constantly dashing from one
spot to another, fixing lights and wiring speakers. The fluted columns that
rose to the high ceiling resembled, if one was stoned enough, Aubrey
Beardsley's lilies, rising forty feet above the concrete floors.
Lights shows galore lit up every inch of available wall space from a massive
light gantry in the centre of the hall. Underground films, notably the
horrid 'Flaming Creatures', were screened on billowing white sheets taped
with electrician's tape to the scaffolding housing the Alexandra Palace organ.
The center piece was a helter skelter, rented for the night, which people
clambered to the top of and spiralled down, quite exhilirating on acid.
The first of the 40 odd bands, poets, artists and dancers that played that
night was the brilliantly abysmal agit-rockers the Social Deviants , who took
the stage at 8 pm. For the better of the night and morning, two bands played
simultaneously on the two stages, often causing an unexpected merger of
styles but mostly causing a headache as the sound reverberated off the walls.
Some bright light of a chemist had chosen the event as the world premiere of
STP, an insane drug that makes you feel like one of the bulls at Pamplona,
charging around with a head full of steam.
Nonetheless, the mood was very positive, as smiling, colourfully dressed
people endlessly milled with chemical quicksteps from corner to corner of
the vast edifice. A plastic igloo had been set up in one corner, where a
laughing Suzy Creamcheese dispensed banana skin joints, touted for their
hallucinogenic effects. A bitter aftertaste really all it left one with,
though, but the idea was more of a intentional put-on anyhow, and one simply
had to laugh at the incongruity of standing in the midst of this mad, milling
throng smoking a banana!

The acts on hand included American black comedian/activist Dick Gregory, Yoko
Ono, artists Binder Edwards and Vaughn (famous for painting pop stripes on a
Cadillac and displaying it in a gallery), Ron Geesin (who later did the
orchestrations for Pink Floyd's 1970 'Atom Heart Mother'), Barry Fantoni,
Scottish author Alexander Trocchi of 'Cain's Book' fame, Christopher Logue,
poet Michael Horovitz and his New Departures team, the 26 Kingly Street group,
(the brilliantly titled) The Utterly Incredible Too Long Ago To Remember
Sometimes Shouting at People, Alexis Korner, Champion Jack Dupree, Graham
Bond, Ginger Johnson and his African conga drummers, Savoy Brown, 117, The
Pretty Things, the proto-punk band The Flies, The Purple Gang, Crazy World
Of Arthur Brown, The Soft Machine and top billed, the Pink Floyd.

Mick Farren of the Deviants, said, 'It was damned good, the Alexandra Palace
was such a beautiful place anyway. And there were mounds of speakers and
light. And everybody who had been fucking around in a small environment got
to go completely nuts. The only thing was that there wasn't much the power
in either the lights or the sound, so it all became a blur, but there was
lots of stuff happening. There were about 10,000 in the audience and a
certain kind of exponential curve seemed to be setting in, which led some
people to believe that we would now conquer the planet.'

Peter Jenner remembers the 14-hour Technicolor Dream: 'That really was a
psychedelic experience. That really was the most psychedelic experience that
I've ever been to. At least half the audience were doing acid. I was doing
acid. We'd had to take a long drive to get there from a gig in Holland, and
I did the last bit of the drive in the van. We dropped in at home and I did
some acid before we went, and by the time I got to Alexandra Palace the old
acid was beginning to go and trying to drive the van was getting quite
exciting.
'It started coming on as we were being directed in. I had to steer the van
in through something very tiny with lots of people wandering around
absolutely out of their crust.' Nick Mason stated, 'We'd played a gig in
Holland that same night and we didn't get to Alexandra Palace till three in
the morning...More like, 'Someone take me home now, please.'

Syd wandered through the crowd, tripping on LSD, the endlessly milling crowd
sweeping slowly and curiously up and down the vast, airy expanses of the
Alexandra Palace. They would pause to see the light shows flickering on the
dancers, or the helter skelter ride in the centre of the hall or the punters
climbing the scaffolding to peer into the pip organ that was being repaired.
Hoppy had to stop the bands and make an impassioned announcement, asking
them to kindly get off. The light bulb installation, a billboard arranged on
a stage, read out handy sound bites in lights, like 'Vietnam is a sad trip.'

Nick Jones of the Melody Maker noted, 'There was (a lot of) noise, and the
Alexandra Palace wasn't the best place for acoustics, most of the sound
echoing up into the high dome and away.' Some people spent the whole night in
one corner, watching the light shows, or climbing on the scaffolding. Others
decamped to one corner, where they laid their coats on the hard floor and
lay down, staring at the ceiling and its acid-induced arabesques, chatting,
sleeping or snogging. There were a lot of people milling about who were very
straight, wearing suits and ties, looking slightly at a loss. One
Underground luminary recalls, 'One of the organisers, who was gay, spent the
whole time under one of the stages having sex with his motorbike boys, for
hours and hours.'

Joe Boyd said, 'The 14 Hour Technicolor Dream was great, though I don't
remember it too clearly. The Alexandra Palace was a big open hall. I was a
bit stoned and had been up all night because we had had UFO the night before.'
DJ John Peel said, 'It was like paradise, it was wonderful. You spent a lot
of time rushing around saying, 'Brian Jones is here, Hendrix is here, where,
where?' Rushing around to see famous people; you were still that much of a
dick head. But it was just a great event. All these bands came on, a lot of
them were awful. There were a few that were really good, but it was the sense
of community, of occasion, the sense that anything was possible.'

Yoko Ono staged a Happening in the style of the Fluxus events she'd been
involved with in New York in the early 1960s. A model, quite stoned, was
seated on a step ladder with a blazing spotlight shining on her. Audience
members were handed a pair of scissors, outfitted with a microphone plugged
into the sound system, and instructed to snip off her clothes. Bit by bit her
clothes fell away, with a crowd of bemused (largely male) punters swarming
around her. Some looked on lecherously, but most just seemed confused. The
sound of the amplified scissors echoed across the hall until the model sat,
in all her glory, completely deshabile.

Keith Rowe, who performed with AMM that night, says 'I remember the 14 Hour
Technicolor Dream as very violent. There was violence towards Yoko quite
often when she performed those pieces with the men ripping away her pants,
I found it unpleasant. A quite powerful emotion. The violence shown to her
was quite out of order. She had racism and sexism against her. Even in 1996
it would probably be illegal to go on-stage and take someone's clothes off,
but with a pair of amplified scissors, its possible.'

'I don't have particularly good memories of the 14 Hour Technicolor Dream,'
says Peter Wynne-Wilson. 'I can't quite picture the scene, I can remember
being up scaffolding there and I can remember someone doing watch-glass
overhead projections. Roger Waters was in a bit of a state about something.
I can remember taking equipment up, but I don't remember doing any lights
there. There was fairground stuff, a lot of drugs, a LOT of drugs. I can
remember thinking that the drug situation had got extremely messy and
perverted because there were people completely in a state because of drink
and drugs. And it seemed to me to be a real falling apart, I didn't like it
at all.'

Miles says, 'The 14 Hour Technicolor Dream was quite boring by virtue of the
fact that it went on for 14 hours. There is a limit to how many dodgy bands
you can listen to, and it was also cold. There weren't many things to do,
and there was nowhere to sit except on the floor. Not very nice, but it was
a heavy socialising scene. Obviously the more people you know the better time
you had. I knew a tremendous number of the people there, so I had a
tremendous time. It's improved with age, at the time I never saw it as
anything fantastic. Only later on did it start to take on a life of its own,
whereas with the Albert Hall poetry reading, that was a significant event.
The 14 Hour Technicolor Dream was no different than a UFO, only a big one;
and I would have preferred UFO anytime.'

The Soft Machine took the stage. Daevid Allen said, 'I had found a miner's
helmet with a lamp set above the brow. Robert Wyatt had set his drums
sideways and Kevin Ayers was wearing makeup. The stages were set at opposite
end of the cavernous venue facing each other, and more often than not two
bands were playing at once. We only heard the band opposite us when we
stopped, so it was supportable...just. After we had finished I wandered
about amongst the huge crowd. All my life I had felt myself to be an outside,
a freak, totally at odds with my time. Now, suddenly, I realised for the
first time that I was not alone. I was surrounded by thousands of other
versions of myself. I was part of a tribe, a movement, a gigantic soul. We
looked around and saw ourselves reflected in multiples and we felt our power
to change the world.
'This was the beginning of a peaceful revolution! As this realisation took
hold of my entire being I became aware of a celestial orchestra playing over
a slow beat. I was drawn to the far stage where, unopposed by a simultaneous
band, a group of slightly embarrassed musicians played symphonic slide
guitar under the camouflage of vividly hypnotic light projections. From the
edge of the stage I watched, fascinated, as a young guy with mad staring
eyes stroked his guitar with metal objects. The music thus created was
almost Wagnerian in its emotional power. It welled up, expanding through the
swirl of liquid light....'
This was a life changing moment for Daevid Allen, who henceforth adapted
Barrett's glissando technique, and refined over a 30 year stretch with
various incarnations of Gong. It many ways Gong, which still exists today,
is the most direct remaining link to Syd Barrett and his music. Barrett's
humour, guitar style and approach all live on in Gong.

Colin Turner, the one-time Mod who had found a portal into a new world at UFO,
was on hand, 'Then the dawn arrived in a triumphant pink hue, the light came
cascading in from the huge windows and amidst this awesome display of nature
Pink Floyd took the stage. They were wearing outfits with flared trousers and
satin shirts that I had not seen them wear before. People began to awake and
hold hands as the first notes of 'Astronomy Domine' reverberated through the
massive hall.

'The atmosphere was electric. There was an extraordinary connection between
the band and the audience. Then the magic happened. Syd's mirror-disc
telecaster caught the dawns pink light. Syd noticed this and with drug-filled
eyes blazing, he made his guitar talk louder and louder, higher and higher as
he reflected the light into the eyes of his audience and christened those of
us lucky enough to be there, followers of Pink Floyd for life.'

Peter Jenner said, 'The band wanted to go on stage just as dawn was breaking,
which they did and it was incredible. The band played at dawn with all the
light coming through the glass at the Palace, the high point of the
psychedelic era for me. It was a perfect setting, everyone had been waiting
for them and everybody was on acid; that event was the peak of acid use in
England...Everybody was on it: the bands, the organisers, the audience, and
I certainly was.'

Robert Wyatt: 'The Floyd played at 4 in the morning. It must have been one of
the greatest gigs they ever did, and Syd played with a slide and it
completely blew my mind, because I was hearing echoes of all the music I'd
ever heard, with bits of Bartok and god-knows-what. I don't understand why
nobody else has ever attempted to do it since. Anyway, I thought I'd better
investigate it.'

Miles memorably wrote, 'Then there was a movement through the crowd and
everyone turned to look at the huge east windows. They were glowing with the
first faint approaches of dawn. At this magic moment of frozen time the Pink
Floyd came on. Their music was eerie, solemn, and calming. After a whole
night of frolicking and festivities and acid came the celebration of the dawn.
A lot of people held hands with their neighbours. The Floyd were probably not
that good but in the moment they were superb. They gave voice to the feelings
of the crowd. Syd's eyes blazed as his notes soared up into the strengthening
light. As the dawn was reflected in his famous mirror- disc Telecaster. Then
came the rebirth of energy, another day, and with the sun a burst of dancing
and enthusiasm. It was quite an event.'

Robert Wyatt said, 'The Floyd had those pyramids as far as I can recall.
They were doing very slow tunes.' The songs they played at the 14 Hour were
slow, and with good reason, Syd was tired, very tired, and tripping too.
It was at moments like this when one's grip on reality begins to loosen.

Daevid Allen spoke of the uncomfortably eerie vibe as the Pink Floyd played,
'the glissando guitar stroker looked as though he was not there. It wouldn't
be long before he wasn't.'

'Shadowy and ghostly,' is how Peter Whitehead remembers Syd at this time.
'Syd was already starting to cultivate this as a deliberate image. It was
partially the way he functioned with people and also as a means of
self-protection. He never found it easy to communicate with people.'
Syd's mystical vibe was partially the result of the glassy eyed distance of
the cannabis and LSD head, but also a strategy to beguile while
simultaneously creating distance.

Miles says, 'Syd wasn't that different than quite a few other people around
at the time until he started to burn himself up with acid. There were a lot
of people around like that by that time. Acid was Syd's drug of choice. He
had a real twinkle of the eye which later came to be a bit mystical. Again
that became quite a common thing.'

Daevid Allen said, 'Mostly Syd Barrett sat around looking completely manic
with staring eyes. In fact, it was very fashionable for everyone to sit
around with staring eyes, like everyone was demented and totally out of
their minds.'

Mark Boyle noted, 'People really did believe that people who took drugs were
pioneers of inner space.' The idea was popularised by Timothy Leary, as well
as Alex Trocchi who wrote in the early sixties about drug users being
'cosmonauts of inner space'. It was an unfortunate mythologisation of drug
use, giving a romantic veneer to burning your brain out.

Whitehead told Record Collector that signs of Syd's impending breakdown
'had been evident for a while, especially as I got the whole inside story
from Jenny Spires, who was a bit cagey but it was clear to us all that he
might not hold it together. He was just out of it, around the clock,
every day. When it reached his stage efforts, it was clearly the beginning
of the end.'
The 14 Hour Technicolor Dream was the last time Whitehead ever saw Syd.

Peter Whitehead went around with his cameras, capturing vignettes of the new
hip aristocracy. But also vivid snaps of a lovely girl with a flower which
she twirls under her nose, her eyes wide with placid contentment, heavy with
mascara like Twiggy's. She seems the embodiment of the naive, fleeting purity
of flower power. Flowers blooming in explosive colour, beguiling those who
see them. The threat that they may be trampled into dust later detracts
nothing from their beauty, it even enhances it because it emphasizes their
ephemeral fragility, their momentary, transitory exquisiteness.

Thirty years on, the image of that girl, frozen on video raises the questions
of where did the flower children go to. Did she finish her studies, drop out
and follow the hippie trail to Marrakech or Kathmandu, marry a stockbroker,
become a feminist or a radical, overdose alone? If you saw her on the street
today would she at all recognisable as the gentle flower child she was then?
With her she took the spirit of the times, and one wonders what she did with
it. Does she reach for it when she opens a box in the back of her closet,
where the Rolling Stones' 'High Tides & Green Grass' LP sits alongside a
faded puce scarf from Biba, and in the yellowed pages of the OZ
'School kids' issue, a pressed flower, dried and preserved, with a shadow
of its former majesty.

The International Times summed up soon after by saying, 'The beautiful scene
at the benefit at the Alexandra Palace on the 29th seems long ago when
considered in the light of all that has happened since then.....One became
aware, through the collecting of all these people, of just how much beauty
and force there is here. And since the benefit there is a difference in
London, a lot of people are speaking to a lot of people whom they only stared
at before. We all know what they are talking about, and its not pop music
or dances and all night raves.'

Over 700 tickets were stolen from a car in Notting Hill Gate a few days
before the event, and precious little of the funds ever found their way back
to the organisers. The trusting ways of the Underground were ill equipped
for the harsh rigours of business. Like the Albert Hall poetry reading
before it, the diverting of the proceeds would create a lot of finger
pointing and animosity within the Underground.

The Sunday Mirror noted, 'The whole thing was rather like the last struggle
of a doomed tribe to save itself from extinction.' Nick Jones wrote in a
summary for the Melody Maker: 'The audience were quite happy looning about,
looking at other's clothes, eating, sleeping, dancing and just freaking out,
doing whatever they damn well wanted. There was a constant supply of films,
slides, joss sticks, sounds, chants, or freakers doing acrobatics on the
scaffolding.....It was just a nice happening. It was fascinating, because
people are fascinating, and it takes a long while to get through 7,000 of
them. I found the Dream a most absorbing experience.'

Hoppy says, 'The 14 Hour Technicolor Dream was a big event and a financial
disaster. Most people were on drugs of one sort or another. It was a crest of
a wave. It wasn't fully understood, but it was a landmark event.' There
seems to be a collective amnesia about the event. No one can remember but a
few glimpses and they're all different. 'Everyone who was involved has a
different story, and they are all true. It's one of those paradoxes. There
are lots of lots of people who say, 'I organised the 14 Hour Technicolor
Dream.' This is what I mean about memory, what is the past? The 14 Hour
Technicolor Dream is a prime example of how memory gives the opportunity for
many people to claim it was their event. Many people claim it was their
event. We all claim it was our event.
'Everyone can claim a piece of it, if they feel it is important. It's rather
like this dream I had where I'm walking in the woods and come across a
clearing where there is a box. I look inside it and pick up this thing I see
inside. I look at it, and I can't see it. There is something there, but I
can't see what it is. And it's like a metaphor or analogy for the 14 Hour
Technicolor Dream. Everybody thinks they know what it was about, but when
you look at it, there's something that you can't find out about it. It's
hidden and occluded. And people who are looking for it will never find it.
It's a cultural memory, and all the accounts are true and conflict with each
other.'

   _____//  Carolismo con delicadeza.       º /----·___________\\ /--------½

  \---------½

Como hacer para amar a alguien a quien nunca viste? Como hacer para amar a
alguien que hace 2 dias que conoces. Como hacer para amar a alguien a quien
quien probablemente nunca veas ni sientas?
Quien puede entender que tengan tanto en comun dos personas que viven tan
lejos, en lugares tan distintos. Como entender que una mera casualidad la
trajo hasta mi, aunque ella dice que no existen las casualidades. Podria
considerarse una especie de regalo divino, pero proveniente de un dios con
un sentido muy negro del humor, que la pone tan lejos de mi. Trato de
entender eso, pero no puedo, y es al contrario, empiezan a surgir en mi mente
mas dudas. Y ya quisiera estar con ella muchas horas para poder hablar.
Y aun asi el idioma seria un problema, y ambos detestamos eso, pero no
podemos hacer nada. Me siento muy contento, pero a la vez es como una
puñalada en el corazon. Hubiese sido mejor que el destino no nos juntase?
Que nos mantuviese en secreto el uno del otro, para que la que la distancia
que nos separa no nos lastimase?
No puedo decir de alguna manera si estoy enamorado, pero hay una conexion,
un vinculo muy fuerte en la manera de hablar, de pensar, de sentir.
Y me duele el hecho de no poder compartirlo en persona,
si viviese cerca no dudaria un instante en ir a verla, conocerla y tratar de
entender ese vinculo que hay. Pero no es asi, cosas extrañas suceden, y creo
que deberia estar contento de tener la posibilidad de conocer a alguien asi. 
Ella odia el dinero, y yo tambien, especialmente porque junto con la distancia
es el factor que nos separa. Ella es de mente muy libre, aunque tal vez no se
de cuenta de eso, agnostica cuando fue criada como musulmana, y ella dice
que no le gusta que la etiqueten, y yo le digo que etiquetar hace a veces la
vida mas facil, y ella, con toda verdad, responde que la facilidad mata el
significado. Quiere dedicar su vida a lo mismo que yo, la biologia.
"El Mundo es un gran laboratorio de Biologia", como dice ella, leo estas
palabras y no puedo mas que sonreir, como puede haber alguien tan parecido a
mi. Ella tambien tiene gran aficion por la cultura oriental, coincidimos en
que el aikido es el mejor arte marcial sin armas, y montones de cosas por el
estilo, no es necesario explicar nada, como ya dijimos en una ocasion,
tenemos una mente compartida. Ella es de caracter relajado, y por eso adora
a los hippies, yo tambien, y exactamente por lo mismo, su vision tan distinta
a la que se tiene por lo general del mundo los hace grandes, y su creencia de
"Hay una forma mejor para todo" es una luz en las mentes. Ella se viste como
hippie, a veces, y aunque yo no lo hago, amo ese tipo de actitud hacia la vida.
Veo que de alguna manera nos complementamos, ella con una tendencia hacia la
vida, yo con una tendencia mas hacia la muerte, pero ambos con algo en comun,
sabemos que no hay una sola forma para ser feliz, pero no estamos seguros si
lo que elegimos es lo correcto.

                  -\-*-*-++++__+++_--isnt it good to be lost in the woods?.












                                                --<-<<-<-<-<-<-<<<<<<<<
saborear la ciudad,
oler la triztesa,
pensar en la risa.
mirar para el costado,
mostrar la indiferencia,
correr de la indiferencia.
entriztecer por ella, 
sentir en el pecho esa cosquilla dolorosa
sentir en los ojos la verguenza.

pensar en la ciudad,
 en aquel pajarito,
 'pobre. con este ruido debe ser un infierno'

mirar el suelo, ver pies, tantas patitas, tantos zapatos...
tantas historias perdidas en el suelo..
y las baldosas,
verlas con la masa negra que antes era chicle,
 la notita con el telefono, 
la hoja resfriada.
y ya casi es de dia, no pasaranon ni 15 minutos, pero ya casi es de dia..
y uno no sabe, uno revuelve con los ojos uno escarba en los demas..
y uno sigue sin saber..
      
sin entender
           y sin un peso
como para comprar las soluciones que venden..

   y que suerte no tener un peso!
   y tener que buscar la solucion
         preguntandole a las baldosas, 

               a los zapatos,
    
             al carton gris que envuelve a los nidos de personas, 
          
            a las lagrimas timidas,

          a los esbozos de idea,

           al papelito con el telefono,

            al dia que ya se va,
          
              a los ojos de alguien que llora.

 Retiro, plena tarde volviendose noche, dos cafes, una larva (B) y
un psicotico esquizofrenico al cual llamaremos D.R., o por su handle,
aneurisma.
 Luego de charla y mas charla, sobre cosas que realmente no importan ahora,
un silencio irrumpio el salon y se mantuvo asi hasta ver deslizandose por
la mesa una hoja de papel que Aneurisma entregaba a la larva, para su
posterior edicion-publicacion en alguna gacetilla underground barata que
no coincida plenamente con los sentimientos del autor en cuestion.
 La persona dio un sorbo, enciendose cigarro y salio corriendo.
Y la larva tuvo que pagar los cafes.

                                        **eL bAUl dE lAS cOSAS viEjiTAS.


Si cada Humano es un mundo y todos viven en uno, -de que forma podrían no
chocarse entre si?-. Pues nada debería llevarnos a pensar que el hecho de
cargar con un mundo, signifique que todos tengan el mismo tamaño, sin contar
que interactúen unos con otros, el espacio que se comparte cuando muchos
interactúan puede ser tan grande como para que todos conformen al mas grande 
y material, llamado planeta tierra. Se que usar términos como "mucho" puede
ser engañoso, es una comparación, es algo poco exacto... y lo que pretendo es
aclarar mis ideas, y que a su vez te sea entretenido.
La forma mas practica de no colisionar nuestras ideas seria que sean todas
iguales, pero afortunadamente el ser Humano es tremendamente complicado desde
nuestra óptica de tal, y tremendamente fácil cuando nos elevamos a un estado
etéreo casi tácito y un poco divino.
Pues de tanto querer diferenciarse, terminamos siendo originalmente iguales.
Y si, podes decirme que existen categorías, o clases de similitudes. Que
los intelectuales, los de clase media, los cazadores, las amas de casa, los
dark, los arquitectos. Pero sintiéndose lejano a estas clasificaciones, uno
ve que todos apuntan a una vida en la cual quieren ser notorios, ya sea por
construir un rascacielos, o por tener el aspecto mas mortuorio de todo el
boliche. Pero no soy mas que cualquiera como para hacer tal comparación,
no me compete, es mas, siquiera la aceptaría, pues un rascacielos se merece
mas admiración de mi parte que un rostro mortuorio... o no es así?. Que
confuso podría decir. Pero me rebajo aun mas a la condición humana y
recapacito. Si yo como juez y jurado de mi pensar, tengo mas interés en
aquel rostro, ya sea por curiosidad, por artista, o por ignorante critica a
lo diferente, entonces si existiría una diferencia entre una "profesión" y
la otra, -una profunda puede ser la diferencia?...- pues tanto como le
parezca a cada individuo.
Apunto mi forma de vivir a mi única aceptación, pues de ceder y ser
manipulado por la visión de cada ser que me afecte emocionalmente, terminaría
siendo un ser agradable para todos menos para mi, y comenzaría siendo una
persona insegura, hueca, y sin una personalidad digna de mi paz interior.

Waffle / Introduction to the Network - Version 1.65
(C) Copyright 1992 Darkside International, All Rights Reserved.

C O N T E N T S

          I   Introduction
         II   Finding a Connection
        III   Get in a Domain - optional
         IV   Mail to Outside Networks
	  V   Further Information

I N T R O D U C T I O N

   Waffle was designed to connect to the UUCP network, which is a
   network of many thousands of machines, the majority of them running
   some variety of Unix. These systems send and receive electronic
   mail, and many are also part of Usenet, which is a large informal
   message system.

   The UUCP network is in turn connected to a larger "world network",
   consisting of several thousand networks interconnected with the
   Domain Name system (DNS). The flexibility of the Domain Name System
   makes it possible to exchange messages with people on other
   networks such as the Internet, BITNET, Compuserve, Fidonet, MCIMAIL,
   plus a good variety of other systems.


F I N D I N G   A   C O N N E C T I O N

   Locating a connection for a news or mail feed is a chicken & egg
   problem -- usually it is necessary to request via E-Mail, and doing
   so requires access to the network. Places to look:

   %  Systems listed in the NIXPUB listing

      There are approximately one hundred Public Access Unix systems
      in the United States, which are available to the general public
      as dialup shell or BBS machines. A list of these systems is
      posted on a regular basis to the pubnet.nixpub newsgroup and also
      crossposted to alt.bbs and comp.misc.

      Many of these systems may be able to provide small Usenet
      systems a mail feed, and some will also be able to provide some
      sort of limited or full newsfeed. A few NIXPUB sites charge a
      small fee (which is reasonable to pay for costs) for newsfeeds.
      Be forewarned that if you have a lowspeed modem (such as 2400)
      your choices are much more limited than if you own a Telebit
      Trailblazer modem.

   %  Local colleges or universities

      Small colleges or universities with a few existing connections
      are occasionally able to permit new sites to connect. Quite
      often, however, the college has overextended their facilities
      or has too many UUCP connections (Rutgers, for instance, would
      be a poor choice to seek such a connection).

      Remember, college system administrators are under no obligation
      to do so and must do this in addition to other pressing tasks.

   %  Sites one hop off the backbone

      Most large sites, sometimes known as backbone sites, are not
      able to give feeds to small sites. However, hosts one hop away
      from backbone sites often are able to accommodate the needs of
      small systems. The best way to locate these systems are to check
      the UUCP maps in your area, or ask around.

   %  Pay services

      There are several systems that offer mail or news connections
      for money. Foremost among these is UUNET Communications, Inc.,
      whose machine uunet.uu.net is the most well connected system
      on the planet. The charge is generally about $30/month plus an
      additional time charge. Further information can be had from

	UUNET Communications, Inc.
	PO Box 2685
	Fairfax VA 22031 USA
	+1 703 764 9789

	uunet-request@uunet.uu.net

      There are other systems that will offer similar services, and
      we will add entries on request.


S U B M I T   A   U U C P   M A P   E N T R Y

   All machines connecting to the UUCP network should submit
   a UUCP map to the map coordinator, <uucpmap@rutgers.edu>. The
   purpose of these maps is to facilitate finding the fastest
   path between any two systems, and also to prevent duplicate
   names that would cause mail to be lost.

   Maps are posted to comp.mail.maps newsgroup on a fairly
   regular basis. In addition to the maps, there is a README file
   that documents these details in much more detail -- the
   information here is not enough to construct a full map entry.

   You should obtain this README file from one of your neighbors;
   it is also available on our BBS system +1 408 245 SPAM (as
   the file /files/waffle/uucp-map.txt).

   The basic format of the maps consists of a number of lines
   with a # and a letter, followed by a tab and then information
   corresponding to that letter:

	#N    UUCP name of site
	#S    manufacturer machine model; operating system & version
	#O    organization name
	#C    contact person's name
	#E    contact person's electronic mail address
	#T    contact person's telephone number
	#P    organization's address
	#L    latitude / longitude
	#R    remarks
	#U    netnews neighbors
	#W    who last edited the entry ; date edited
	#
	sitename      .domain
	sitename      remote1(FREQUENCY), remote2(FREQUENCY),
	      remote3(FREQUENCY)

    Here is a sample entry for our mythical "elf" site, just to
    give an idea of what things should look like:

	#N    elf
	#S    Intel 80386 ; Waffle UUCP
	#O    Elf Consulting, Santa Cruz CA
	#C    Floyd R Turbo
	#E    floyd@elf.santa-cruz.ca.us
	#T    +1 408 555 1212
	#P    573 Evans Hall, Berkeley, CA 94720
	#L    37 52 29 N / 122 13 44 W
	#R    We build electronic listening devices & glockenspiels.
	#U    ozone
	#W    elf!floyd (Floyd R Turbo); Tue Jul 24 22 03:35:16 PDT 1990
	#
	elf	ozone(HOURLY), frutti(DAILY)

   Although systems in registered domains are not required to
   submit UUCP maps, it is highly recommended. Again we must stress
   the need to obtain the UUCP maps README file before attempt
   construction of your map entry, or have one of your neighbors
   submit one for you.


G E T   I N   A   D O M A I N   -   o p t i o n a l

   The main difficulty with the UUCP maps is that it has a flat
   namespace - once a name is taken, it cannot be used by others.
   After a while, all the good names are taken. Also, large
   organizations tend to have trouble inventing names that identify
   with that organization; this combined with the 7 character
   limit on names creates very strange names.

   All these problems have been solved by the use of the DNS,
   the Internet Domain Name System. An organization can apply for
   registration in a toplevel domain and place all their machines
   within their domain. Toplevel domains include

	.COM	Commercial Domain
	.GOV	Government Domain
	.ORG	Organization Domain
	.MIL	Military Domain

   Also there exists a toplevel domain consisting of two characters
   for many countries, examples of which include

	.US	United States
	.CA	Canada
	.DE	Germany
	.UK	United Kingdom

   These domains use the standard two character ISO abbreviations,
   with the exception of UK for some strange reason.

   Registration within the .COM, .GOV, or .ORG is not limited
   to entities in the United States, regardless of what you are
   told by your PTT or anyone else. We urge anyone who can to
   has the resources to register in one of those toplevel domains.

   There are a number of ways to get yourself located in
   a domain of one sort or another:

   %  Find an Internet Forwarder and Nameservers

      Locate a willing forwarder on the Internet to forward your
      mail to you via UUCP. Note that the presence of .COM .GOV or
      .ORG does not necessarily mean that the system is on the
      Internet. You must also locate two nameservers on the Internet
      (one of which can also be your forwarder).

      This process can be fairly painful (we went through it to
      get our .darkside.com domain registered). Paperwork must be
      sent to the NIC (Network Information Center) and processed
      in order for you to obtain a registered domain.

   %  UUNET Domain Registration

      For a $30 fee, UUNET will register your domain for you, and
      provide NS services to direct your traffic to a desired
      Internet host (possibly UUNET). There is no charge for this
      if you are a UUNET customer.

      This is the EASIEST way for you to register a domain. Further
      information may be obtained by contacting

	domain-request@uunet.uu.net

      A number of systems using Waffle have done this, and they
      appear to be satisfied with the service.

   %  Domain Parks

      If you do not want to go through the hassle of registering a
      domain, you can join a domain park. Domain Parks are regional
      areas that one can usually join by just asking. Often these
      are on state boundaries, though this is not necessarily the case.

      A few, but certainly not all, domain parks that
      we have discovered include:

        LONESTAR.ORG       Region:  Republic of Texas
                           Contact: Currently in limbo - wait & see

        MI.ORG             Region:  Michigan
                           Contact: Bob Leffler <bob@rel.mi.org>

        MN.ORG             Region:  Minnesota
                           Contact: Shane McCarron <abby@mn.org>

        PDX.COM            Region:  Portland Oregon
                           Contact: Dale Weber <dalew@twiki.PDX.COM>

        SF-BAY.ORG         Region:  San Francisco Bay Area
                           Contact: Scott Mueller <scott@zorch.SF-BAY.ORG>

        SOCAL.COM          Region:  Southern California
                           Contact: postmaster@socal.com

        SUBLINK.ORG        Region:  Italy
                           Contact: Postmaster <postmaster@sublink.sublink.org>

        WA.COM             Region:  Washington State
                           Contact: info@nwnexus.wa.com

        WAFFLE.ATL.GA.US   Region: 404, 706 Area Code Waffles
                           Contact: uucp-request@waffle.atl.ga.us

      Most of these will require you to establish a connection
      to receive forwarded mail. We do not endorse any of these
      domains listed, and can't take responsibility for errors
      contained here.

      People in Germany might look into the German Subnet,
      or <sub.org>. Similarly, people in Italy might look into
      the Italian subnet, <sublink.org>. These networks are
      separate from the government bureaucracies and we see this
      as a healthy trend.

   %  The .US Domain

      If you have an Internet forwarder but do not wish to find
      nameservers yourself (or pay UUNET $30 to do it for you)
      consider registering your site in the .US domain.

      Hosts in the .US domain are <name>.<city>.<state>.US,
      where <city> is either the name of your town or the Western
      Union abbreviation of it. Examples of systems in the .US
      domain are

	fernwood.mpk.ca.us
	killer.dallas.tx.us

      It is very easy to register in the .US domain; all that
      really needs to be done is mail your request to the .US
      registrar, <COOPER@ISI.EDU>. A form is available for this
      purpose either from <COOPER@ISI.EDU>, by anonymous FTP
      at NIC.DDN.MIL (in NETINFO:US-DOMAIN.TXT) or for download
      at +1 408 245 SPAM in /files/waffle/us-domain.txt.

      We are also willing to mail copies of this file on request,
      just ask for "US-DOMAIN.TXT" file.

   %  Hang off someone's Domain

      A company, college, or university may permit you to become a
      member of their domain. This may be true if you are an
      employee of the organization; if not, don't count on it..


M A I L   T O   O U T S I D E   N E T W O R K S

   Mail gateways exist between the Internet systems and a
   variety of outside networks. Depending on your system, you
   may be able to use the @'notation or you may have to
   rewrite the address form given into a bangpath. Some gateways
   to the major networks include:

   %  BITNET

      The BITNET (for Because It's Time) is a collection of large IBM
      computers connected mostly with 9600 baud leased lines. Many
      small colleges and government organizations are part of BITNET.

	USER%SYSTEM.BITNET@cunyvm.cuny.edu

      People on BITNET who need to get mail to the outside should
      contact their system administrators for more details.

   %  Compu$erve

      Compuserve (also known as CIS) is not a true network, but it
      has a large number of customers and offers electronic mail and
      a number of public forums somewhat similar to Usenet.

      To get mail into Compuserve from the outside world, change the
      comma in the CIS address into a period, and use this format:

	77612.65535@compuserve.com

      To send mail from compuserve to the outside, ">INTERNET:"
      must be placed before the address, for example

	>INTERNET:dell@vox.darkside.com

      There is no way to guess someone's CIS id number, and there
      are no gateways for CIS public forums.

   %  FidoNET

      FidoNET consists of about 7,000 machines, most of them IBM PC
      compatible. It is the world's largest microcomputer network,
      and is hierarchically arranged into zones, regions, nets, systems,
      and points. A sample address is

	James Dean at 1:350/12.2

      where "1" is the zone (1 is the North American Continent),
      350 is the net, 12 is the machine, and 2 is the point (which is
      a "private" system hanging off someone's machine). It should be
      noted that most systems are not points.

      The address above cannot be handled by most networks since
      it is syntactically illegal outside of FidoNET. Translating into
      a more conventional form, this becomes

	James.Dean@p5.f12.n350.z1.fidonet.org

      although if the point at the end was not present, it would be

	James.Dean@f12.n350.z1.fidonet.org

      A complete listing of all nodes is available in a list
      known as the NODELIST, distributed to Fido systems.

      There are some similar networks based on Fido standards, but
      they are not easily reachable from the outside world at this time.
      This will be changing in the near future, however.

   %  MCIMAIL

      MCI operates an electronic mail service called MCIMAIL. Mail
      can be sent to their customers using the form

	2148871@mcimail.com

      Apparently, customers with "low" numbers have been with MCIMAIL
      the longest.


F U R T H E R   I N F O R M A T I O N

All this information might be a bit overwhelming to those with no
background in this area. Two books we have found to be very helpful are:

	Using UUCP and Usenet; Grace Todino;
	O'Reilly & Associates. ISBN 0-937175-10-2

	Managing UUCP and Usenet; Tim O'Reilly and Grace Todino;
	O'Reilly & Associates. ISBN 0-937175-09-9

Note:   The new edition of Managing UUCP and Usenet omits
        Waffle from the DOS UUCP section. Please feel free to
        notify nuts@ora.com of their glaring oversight.

Both are "Nutshell" handbooks. An 800 number they list is
1-800-338-NUTS; 981 Chestnut Street Newton MA 02164 USA.

We have no affiliation with this publisher.

--
dell@vox.darkside.com

William Burroughs -- A Sketch
John C. Kramer, M.D. Associate Professor, Department of Psychiatry,
   University of California of Medicine, Irvine, California 92717.
~Journal of Psychoactive Drugs~ Vol. 13(1):95-97 Jan-Mar, 1981
A recolection of a talk with William S. Burroughs.
O.C.R. by Dr. Rat, I.C.R. Laboratories Inc. 1992



What about psychedelics?

``Well, cannabis is useful. When you're stuck and don't know where you're
going you smoke cannabis and then you see four or five ways the narrative
can go. No one is going to become a writer from taking any of these drugs
but they can get beneficial material from them.

``I don't like any of the stronger psychedelics. I would never take LSD...
I hate it.''

``You've tried it?'' (Obviously.)

``I've tried it. I just hate it. I don't like the feeling.... It makes me
nervous. My coordination isn't good and there's a metallic taste in my
mouth and there's nothing I like about it. I've taken mescaline,
psilocybin. The only one I've been able to use with consistency is
cannabis.''

``Has anything useful come to you with mescaline or psilocybin?''

``Yes, but mostly of an unpleasant nature. There is one interesting one
though, yage', but I've never been able to get any since I left South
America. There's ~Banisteriopsis~ in it; that's the main ingredient but not
the only one. The medicine men use it to potentiate their powers, to locate
lost objects and that kind of thing. But I'm not impressed much by their
performance. Everybody has telepathic experiences all the time. These
things are not rare. It's just an integral part of life. The faculty is
probably increased to some extent by any consciousness expanding drug.''


We talked dope talk some more. Opium smoking and opium dreams. Life in
Morocco and how it was the old people, not the young ones, who smoked
cannabis. And about majoun, marijuana candy. And I told him about khat in
Arabia. And he told me about the lies that Anslinger spread. And we told
each other about Hasan-i-Sabah and how the ~haschischins~ were not driven
to murder because they were stoned. And he got back to his apomorphine
stories.

Notes for lecture (on New US Prosody to Marxist Literary Conference)
dec 1962.


1) The reason for changes - increased depth of perception on nonverbal-
onconceptual level.
        a) Spontaneous natural visionary
        b) Organized experiment in consciousness:
                1. thru jazz ecstacy & mantras
                2. thru that Electronic Machinery
                3. thru drugs
                4. tantra & Zen meditation.
Consequences in poetic composition: an attempt to include more
simultaneous perceptions and relate previously unrelated (what were
thought irrelevant) occurrences.
 By means of:
        1) Reliance on spontaneous writing to capture the whole mind
           of the Poet - not just what he thinks he should think with
           his front brain.
        2) Interest in the      awkwardness
                                accidents
                                rhythm
           jump of perception from one thing to another breaking
                                synctactical order
                                punctuation order
                                logical orders
                                old narrative order
                                meaning order.
Notations of process of mind
& relative natural process
Uncensored by
        grammar
        syntax
        order

==(fUERA eE.uU. y lA oNu dE iRAk pOR lA dERROTa dE lOS iMPERiALiSTAs)=========

Estados Unidos comenzo la cuenta regresiva para una nueva masacre en Irak,
peor que la perpreto en el a¤o 91.
El primer objetivo de la guerra lo expreso sin vueltas una editorial del
New York Times: "Irak estara controlado por el pu¤o de hierro del ejercito
norteamericano y sus aliados, con una administracion civil 'asesora' iraqui
que ira surgiendo detras de este pu¤o de hierro" (5/2). Tras una victoria
imperialista en Irak, pretenden imponer en Medio Oriente su "solucion" a
la lucha del heroico pueblo palestino, enterrando sus aspiraciones de
libertad nacional, y lograr en la region regimenes titeres de EE.UU. para
controlar las principales reservas petroleras del mundo.
Para intentar convencer a la opinion publica norteamericana y del mundo,
la excusa del ataque imperialista es que Irak posee armas de destruccion
masiva y constituye "un peligro para la paz y seguridad internacional".
Los poseedores de los mas grandes armamentos nucleares y convencionales del
mundo deciden que puede y que no puede tener un peque¤o estado semicolonial.
No obstante ello, los inspectores de armas de la ONU han demostrado la total
falta de "evidencias". Su jefe, Hans Blix, declaro al Consejo de Seguridad
este 14 de febrero "Nosotros no debemos llegar a la conclusion de que (las
armas de destruccion masiva en irak) existen. No obstante, esta posibilidad
puede descartarse". Y aun asi Estados Unidos, secundado por Gran Breta¤a y
Espa¤a, de todos modos ira a la guerra con o sin el aval de las Naciones
Unidas, chantajeando a las principales potencias europeas, Alemania y Francia,
con que, en caso de un triunfo norteamericano contundente quedarian marginadas
del reparto del botin de la posguerra. Y como Francia y Alemania no estan,
por ahora, en condiciones militares de disputar ese botin, se muestran
reticentes a la decision "unilateral" de los norteamericanos y por eso piden
"mas tiempo" para los inspectores de armas de la ONU. Esta es la verdadera
discusion y disputas politicas entre los EE.UU. y las principales potencias
de Europa, que estos ultimos enmascaran, por un problema de conveniencia
para sus apetitos imperialistas, tras una fachada "pacifista" y en nombre
de una "solucion politica" al conflicto. Incluso Francia no descarta "como
ultimo recurso" el uso de la fuerza militar, y que su posicion nada tiene
que ver con el pacifismo lo demuestra su reciente incursion militar
"unilateral" en Costa de Marfil. Y hasta hicieron circular la version de un
plan de instalacion de "cascos azules" para convertir a Irak en un
protectorado de la ONU. Aprovechar las disputas interimperialistas? Si,
pero no para recostarse en n bando imperialista contra el otro, como parecen
promover los dirigentes del Foro Social Mundial reunido en Porto Alegre.
Sino para impulsar la movilizacion independiente. El movimiento antiguerra
no solo debe oponerse y luchar contra la agresion imperialista de Bush y
sus aliados mas cercanos como Blair y Aznar, sino que debe rechazar la
politica imperialista de Alemania y Francia y exigir el retiro de las
misiones e inspectores de la ONU de Irak.

4-7-02                                    

Desde Centenario no se ve hacia adentro: las puertas son de vidrio ahumado.
A la entrada, del aldo de adentro, dos "hermanos" lo reciben a uno con
sonrisas, manos que quieren estrechar la de uno, folletos con la foto algún
sacerdote gordo, micrófono en mano, en la tapa y frases triunfalistas que
completan la hojita doblada en tres. Los hermanos, el hombre de pantalón
gris, camisa blanca y corbata negra, la mujer de pollera gris por debajo de
la rodilla, camisa blanca, sin corbata, ambos de sonrisitas pulcras y miradas
indolentes, se ofrecen para escoltarnos hasta el asiento más cercano posible
al altar. De todos modos, para protejernos de cualquier mal, cada 5 metros
hay un hermano o hermana a ambos lados de las butacas, cuidando a las almas
dolidas que concurren a misa. Mientras el sacerdote se prepara para la quinta
función del día, los cuatro pares de altoparlantes Bose vomitan una
seguidilla de música popular con letras que alaban el amor de Cristo.

huir es la norma mientras titilan
diagramas verdes y azules del gotero

horas, rostros familiares y contar
monedas, sentado en la acera de un
kiosco en quien sabe que parte del
globo terrestre, principalmente hacia
el sur, paises frios y demasiado
oscuros o la plenitud de la calidez
y la buena vibra naciente despues
de las once p.m., los relojes se
empa¤an y se niegan a mostrar la
verdad de las horas, o solo mienten

solo dia en el mismo punto del cosmos,
el ojo perdido, la degradacion
absoluta de mentes en pena buscando

conformando la masa que alimenta
los egos llegando a las cuatro de

inalcanzables.

jovenes de mi generacion..' algun_lado_de_la_costa, 2002.),
poeta de alcantarilla, poeta de plaza urbana, poeta en desdicha, 
poeta y su idea subliminal, poeta y la deforestacion, poeta y recuerdos de
infancia (comparaciones absurdas con el solo hecho de infligir en un medio
particular restante que carece de logica ((claro, que no la necesita)), pero
repercute mediante imagenes falsas, sentimientos irreales, poeta perdido en
combustion de paranoia y estimulantes varios, poeta asesinado por error
(quien dijo era poeta?), poeta dando vida a nuevos estilos, poeta ministro de
economia (que?), poeta y su libertad usurpada, poeta con hijo recien
nacido en brazos, poeta perdido en las inmediaciones que lo rodea,
poeta inocente aprendiendo de la vida, poeta Jesus-Cristo publicando las
ideas mas carentes de contenido y realidad de toda la jodida existencia,
eones y eones por detras, poeta de subte linea A (alimentando su ego perdido
con una manzana), poeta influenciado por el acido ('Si de majestuosas
imagenes acolorales puedo vivir vistiendo el segundo irremplazable, elevacion
sin forma comprometiendome, esbozo de nacion multicolor delante de lo que
podria ser mi Cuerpo soluble delante de -un algo-, empatia y colores efimeros),

            Las drogas en 1999 // en Buenoz Airez // por Rosko.

Nota: este es mi punto de vista, y puede ser una visi¢n equivocada,
      de todas maneras, quiero creer que tengo la suficiente expe
      riencia como para que se tenga en cuenta lo que digo.

  Voy a hablarles de lo que yo v¡ en mi vida desde que empez‚ a hacer
uso de drogas. Esto pas¢ en 1992 cuando yo ten¡a 14 a¤os, y fue para
mi una puerta a un mundo nuevo. Un para¡so propio donde todo era posible.

  Lo que me parece es que en Buenoz Airez, la gente no sabe usar drogas, y
quiz  por una cuesti¢n de instinto, los adolescentes de corta edad (15, 16)
son los que las utilizan (como ya dije, por instinto, miedo o respeto)
de la manera adecuada, es decir, con la solemnidad y conciencia de rito
que las drogas necesitan.

  Lo que yo veo es un uso indiscriminado y una mezcla violenta de diferentes
tipos de drogas, por ejemplo, he visto gente que en una noche ha mezclado narco
ticos (alcohol) +alucinogenos (cannabis, lsd) +exitantes (cocaina). Esto puede
llevar al individuo que lo practica a estados alterados de conciencia realmente
ext ticos pero el entorno que mueve al alienado habitante de Buenos Aires de fin
de siglo, el que lo empuja a esta clase de consumo, es un corrupto "toma y dame"
que nada sabe de ‚xtasis y relaci¢n con lo misterioso; aparte de valerse de la
insatisfacci¢n, el miedo y la decepci¢n para empujar al sujeto a este tipo de
pr cticas; lo que desde ya (por la intervenci¢n del miedo y otros sentimientos
anulantes) destruye la capacidad creativa del drog¢n.

 Esta situaci¢n la pude vivir en carne propia en una plaza, con 7 u 8 personas,
todas bebiendo y fumando, burl ndose de de alguien (por lo general del integran
te mas inteligente o sensible del grupo) y hablando incoherencias sin sentido,
solo para mantener los o¡dos ocupados. Escuchar a otro hablar o hablar uno para
usar los cuerpos y para no oir el buen silencio que dice mucho cuando uno se
droga, es triste y todo un s¡mbolo del mal uso de las drogas.
 Por algo en ingles a estar fumado se le dice "stoned", de piedra, sin poder
hablar. O sin querer; en fin, yo tuve que soportar las burlas de la canalla
por ser el m s sensible del grupo, lugar de donde me fu¡ rapidamente por no
encontrar eco para mis inquietudes art¡sticas y ‚ticas. Quiero recalcar que
por lo general las personas que cargan esta alienacion vergonzosa y triste son
hombres, las mujeres siguen siendo mujeres, y siempre van a estar dispuestas
a contentarse con el devenir de la situaci¢n, o a seguir al primer macho decidi
do que proponga romper con la monoton¡a y el enajenamiento del grupo.

  Hay muchos manejes sucios, vidas que se pierden, gente que se muere de hambre y
tiranos que se llenan los bolsillos, que son los que hacen facil el consumo
de drogas en la Argentina y que son los mismos que crearon la ley de drogas
para rompernos el orto a nosotros, los drogones. Y la gente que consume no sabe
que no es normal esta situaci¢n de que haya tanta variedad y cantidad de droga,
y tan barata. Por eso creo que se tiene que apreciar esta situaci¢n, mas all 
de la parte negativa que menciono. Treinta a¤os atr s la cuesti¢n era muy distin
ta, y hoy, si uno es un poco inteligente, puede aprender mucho de la cultura de
las drogas. Y la gran mayor¡a no se da cuenta de esto, sino que usa las drogas
de la manera que el sistema quiere, para anularse y para llenarle los bolsillos
de plata a quienes nos "gobiernan."

  El fin £ltimo de este manifiesto es eyacular mi decepci¢n y asco por la
escena de las drogas en Buenos Aires. Ya lo dijeron Los Piojos en su tema
"Los Cancheros" no queremos la tuca/ni tu cara de pezcadito regalando premios
desde teve/ solo quieren que te rias/ que triste debe ser". Alla uds. en el uso
que le den a las drogas, pero por si no lo saben, las drogas son s¢lo otra arma
del sistema para destruir nuestra poderosa generaci¢n que tiene todo. Yo fumo
porro, lo cual me gusta y me eleva. Pero me rehuso a pertener a la horrorosa
escena drogona de BsAs, que se dice llamar "LA ONDA" donde unos pocos viven
sorbiendole la sangre y los sesos a los mas inteligentes. Por eso si vas a usar
drogas, seria bueno que te rodees de gente como vos y te cuides de abusar de

con dios, o para el amor con tu compa¤er@. No para discutir quien tiene onda o

                                                   Rosko--El Chaco, 1999.
